restitutio in integrum (to restore parties to their original
position) : the measure of damages is stated to be restitutio in
integrum. In other words the injured party is entitled to be put,
as far as practicable, into the same condition as if the injury
had not been suffered; but the wrongdoer is only liable for such
damages as flow directly from the wrongful act मूल स्थिति में
लाना
